            spectrometer.                                         2093900100015

METHOD     (TOF,TRN) Time of flight, 120 meter flight path,       2093900100018 
             4000 channels, 4 mc/s magnetic tape analyser.        2093900100019 
             Resolution 2.6 nano-sec/meter.                       2093900100020 
ANALYSIS    The total cross section is derived from the thicker   2093900100021 
            sample transmission data between resonance and from   2093900100022 
            thin sample transmission data for the resonance peaks.2093900100023 
           .The total width of each resonance is obtained from    2093900100024 
            the intersection on the G-n, G-t plane of curves      2093900100025 
            from the established methods of analysis              2093900100026 
           (AREA ) area analysis for G-n.                         2093900100027 
           .The transmission area method of Hughes for the        2093900100028 
            thicker sample, and the minimum transmission          2093900100029 
            method of Lynn.                                       2093900100030 
           (SHAPE) Shape analysis was used to determine sigma(0)  2093900100031 
             and total width, for resonances where Doppler        2093900100032 
             broadening is small.                                 2093900100033 
REL-REF    (M,,J.E.Lynn+,J,JNE,4,418,1957) - the minimum          2093900100034 
            transmission method and addition shape analysis       2093900100035 
           (M,,D.J.Hughes,J,JNE,1,237,1955) - the transmission    2093900100036 
            area method                                           2093900100037 
DETECTOR   (SOLST) The neutron booster time-of-flight spectrometer2093900100038 
CORRECTION .Background corrected with an equal thickness of       2093900100039 
            aluminium in beam.                                    2093900100040 
            Above 100 eV self shielding effects are negligible.   2093900100041 
ERR-ANALYS (DATA-ERR) Nothing said about source of uncertainties  2093900100042
